```diff
 	//  - "jobset.x-k8s.io/jobset"
 	Frameworks []string `json:"frameworks,omitempty"`
 }
+
+type QueueVisibility struct {
+	// LocalQueues is configuration to expose the information
+	// about the top pending workloads in the local queue.
+	LocalQueues *LocalQueueVisibility `json:"localQueues,omitempty"`
+
+	// ClusterQueues is configuration to expose the information
+	// about the top pending workloads in the cluster queue.
+	ClusterQueues *ClusterQueueVisibility `json:"clusterQueues,omitempty"`
+
+	// UpdateInterval specifies the time interval for updates to the structure

+	// Defaults to 5s.
+	// +optional
+	UpdateInterval *metav1.Duration `json:"updateInterval,omitempty"`
```

  ```suggestion

  ```
  https://github.com/kubernetes/community/blob/master/contributors/devel/sig-architecture/api-conventions.md#units

- **apis/config/v1beta1/configuration_types.go:250** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-08-21T14:18:53Z
```diff
@@ -224,3 +228,41 @@ type Integrations struct {
 	//  - "jobset.x-k8s.io/jobset"
 	Frameworks []string `json:"frameworks,omitempty"`
 }
+
+type QueueVisibility struct {
+	// LocalQueues is configuration to expose the information
+	// about the top pending workloads in the local queue.
+	LocalQueues *LocalQueueVisibility `json:"localQueues,omitempty"`
+
+	// ClusterQueues is configuration to expose the information
+	// about the top pending workloads in the cluster queue.
+	ClusterQueues *ClusterQueueVisibility `json:"clusterQueues,omitempty"`
+
+	// UpdateInterval specifies the time interval for updates to the structure
+	// of the top pending workloads in the queues.
+	// Defaults to 5s.
+	// +optional
+	UpdateInterval *metav1.Duration `json:"updateInterval,omitempty"`
+}
+
+type LocalQueueVisibility struct {
+	// MaxCount indicates the maximal number of pending workloads exposed in the
+	// local queue status. When the value is set to 0, then LocalQueue visibility
+	// updates are disabled.
+	// The maximal value is 4000.
+	// Defaults to 10.
+	MaxCount int32 `json:"maxCount,omitempty"`
+
+	// MaxPosition indicates the maximal position of the workload in the cluster
+	// queue returned in the head.
+	MaxPosition *int32 `json:"maxPosition,omitempty"`
+}
+
+type ClusterQueueVisibility struct {
+	// MaxCount indicates the maximal number of pending workloads exposed in the
+	// cluster queue status.  When the value is set to 0, then LocalQueue
+	// visibility updates are disabled.
+	// The maximal value is 4000.
```

  The validation code seems to be missing.

- **apis/kueue/v1beta1/clusterqueue_types.go:193** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-08-21T14:20:01Z
```diff
@@ -176,6 +176,28 @@ type ResourceQuota struct {
 // ResourceFlavorReference is the name of the ResourceFlavor.
 type ResourceFlavorReference string
 
+// ClusterQueuePendingWorkload contains the information identifying a pending workload
+// in the cluster queue.
+type ClusterQueuePendingWorkload struct {
+	// Name indicates the name of the pending workload.
+	Name string `json:"name"`
+
+	// Namespace indicates the name of the pending workload.
+	Namespace string `json:"namespace"`
+}
+
+type ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus struct {
+	// Head contains the list of top pending workloads.
+	// +listType=map
+	// +listMapKey=name
+	// +listMapKey=namespace
```

  ```suggestion
  	// +listType=atomic
  ```
  
  The order here matters, so it should not be a map.

- **pkg/config/validation.go:19** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-08-24T14:34:52Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,31 @@
+package config
+
+import (
+	"fmt"
+
+	configapi "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/config/v1beta1"
+)
+
+var (
+	errInvalidMaxValue              = fmt.Errorf("maximum value for QueueVisibility.ClusterQueues.MaxCount must be %d", queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxValue)
+	errInvalidUpdateIntervalSeconds = fmt.Errorf("minimum value for QueueVisibility.UpdateIntervalSeconds must be %d", queueVisibilityClusterQueuesUpdateIntervalSeconds)
+)
+
+const (
+	queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxValue              = 4000
+	queueVisibilityClusterQueuesUpdateIntervalSeconds = 1
+)
+
+func validate(cfg *configapi.Configuration) error {
```

- **pkg/queue/manager.go:604** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-08-24T14:49:39Z
```diff
@@ -547,3 +570,36 @@ func (m *Manager) reportPendingWorkloads(cqName string, cq ClusterQueue) {
 	}
 	metrics.ReportPendingWorkloads(cqName, active, inadmissible)
 }
+
+func (m *Manager) Start(ctx context.Context) error {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithName("clusterQueueSnapshot")
+	ctx = ctrl.LoggerInto(ctx, log)
+
+	ticker := time.NewTicker(
+		time.Duration(m.cfg.QueueVisibility.UpdateIntervalSeconds) * time.Second,
+	)
+	defer ticker.Stop()
+
+	for {
+		select {
+		case <-ctx.Done():
+			log.V(2).Info("Context cancelled; stop doing snapshot of cluster queue")
+			return nil
+		case t := <-ticker.C:
+			m.workloadsStatus = &kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+				Head:           make([]kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload, 0),
+				LastChangeTime: metav1.Time{Time: t},
+			}
+			for _, wl := range m.Snapshot() {
+				m.workloadsStatus.Head = append(m.workloadsStatus.Head, kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload{
+					Name:      wl.Name,
+					Namespace: wl.Namespace,
+				})
+			}
+		}
+	}
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) GetWorkloadsStatus() *kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus {
+	return m.workloadsStatus
```

  the lock mentioned above should be locked for read here.

### Review by [@stuton](https://github.com/stuton) (commented) — 2023-08-25T16:33:42Z

- **pkg/queue/manager.go:604** by [@stuton](https://github.com/stuton) — 2023-08-25T16:33:42Z
```diff
@@ -547,3 +570,36 @@ func (m *Manager) reportPendingWorkloads(cqName string, cq ClusterQueue) {
 	}
 	metrics.ReportPendingWorkloads(cqName, active, inadmissible)
 }
+
+func (m *Manager) Start(ctx context.Context) error {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithName("clusterQueueSnapshot")
+	ctx = ctrl.LoggerInto(ctx, log)
+
+	ticker := time.NewTicker(
+		time.Duration(m.cfg.QueueVisibility.UpdateIntervalSeconds) * time.Second,
+	)
+	defer ticker.Stop()
+
+	for {
+		select {
+		case <-ctx.Done():
+			log.V(2).Info("Context cancelled; stop doing snapshot of cluster queue")
+			return nil
+		case t := <-ticker.C:
+			m.workloadsStatus = &kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+				Head:           make([]kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload, 0),
+				LastChangeTime: metav1.Time{Time: t},
+			}
+			for _, wl := range m.Snapshot() {
+				m.workloadsStatus.Head = append(m.workloadsStatus.Head, kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload{
+					Name:      wl.Name,
+					Namespace: wl.Namespace,
+				})
+			}
+		}
+	}
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) GetWorkloadsStatus() *kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus {
+	return m.workloadsStatus
```

  mutex was added

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2023-08-29T07:54:23Z

First pass, main suggestion is to revisit how the snapshot is taken

- **apis/config/v1beta1/configuration_types.go:243** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-08-29T07:47:24Z
```diff
@@ -226,3 +230,24 @@ type Integrations struct {
 	//  - "kubeflow.org/tfjob"
 	Frameworks []string `json:"frameworks,omitempty"`
 }
+
+type QueueVisibility struct {
+	// ClusterQueues is configuration to expose the information
+	// about the top pending workloads in the cluster queue.
+	ClusterQueues *ClusterQueueVisibility `json:"clusterQueues,omitempty"`
+
+	// UpdateIntervalSeconds specifies the time interval for updates to the structure
+	// of the top pending workloads in the queues.
+	// The minimum value is 1.
+	// Defaults to 5s.
+	UpdateIntervalSeconds int32 `json:"updateIntervalSeconds,omitempty"`
```

  Can we make it `time.Duration`? As we did for `CacheSyncTimeout` or `WaitForPodsReady,Timeout`. It is more flexible.

- **pkg/queue/manager.go:534** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-08-29T07:52:50Z
```diff
@@ -489,6 +530,22 @@ func (m *Manager) DumpInadmissible() map[string]sets.Set[string] {
 	return dump
 }
 
+// Snapshot is a copy of the queues elements and inadmissible workloads list.
+func (m *Manager) Snapshot() []*kueue.Workload {
```

  I would prefer to avoid taking snapshot for all CQ in the same loop. In can be costly if we have many CQs, say 100. It was one of the concerns during the KEP review. 
  
  The proposed solution is to have a fixed pool of workers that do the snapshots based on queue of snapshot tasks. Take a look here: https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/tree/main/keps/168-pending-workloads-visibility#in-memory-snapshot-of-the-clusterqueue. So, the idea is to have `takeSnapshot` function keying by the CQ name. Similarly as it is done for Job controller: https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/blob/master/pkg/controller/job/job_controller.go#L233-L235. Then, we could have a function `enqueueSnapshotDelayed` to schedule taking snapshot after the configured interval.
  
  We may sync up to discuss if there are some complications with this model.

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2023-08-30T13:19:58Z

- **pkg/util/heap/heap.go:175** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-08-30T13:19:54Z
```diff
@@ -169,8 +170,9 @@ func (h *Heap) Len() int {
 	return h.data.Len()
 }
 
-// List returns a list of all the items.
+// List returns a sorted list of all the items.
 func (h *Heap) List() []interface{} {
+	sort.Sort(&h.data)
```

  I don't think we want to sort here. First, IIUC, it can destroy the state of the heap. Second, the sorting should take into account both the heap.items and the inadmissibleWorkloads. Finally, it is preferable to make the sorting and post processing outside of the read lock, to make it as quick as possible.

- **pkg/queue/manager.go:651** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-08-31T08:43:58Z
```diff
@@ -547,3 +594,90 @@ func (m *Manager) reportPendingWorkloads(cqName string, cq ClusterQueue) {
 	}
 	metrics.ReportPendingWorkloads(cqName, active, inadmissible)
 }
+
+func (m *Manager) Start(ctx context.Context) error {
+	defer m.queue.ShutDown()
+
+	queueVisibilityUpdateInterval := time.Duration(m.queueVisibilityUpdateInterval) * time.Second
+
+	for i := 0; i < snapshotWorkers; i++ {
+		go wait.UntilWithContext(ctx, m.takeSnapshot, queueVisibilityUpdateInterval)
+	}
+
+	go wait.UntilWithContext(ctx, m.enqueueSnapshotDelayed, queueVisibilityUpdateInterval)
+
+	<-ctx.Done()
+
+	return nil
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) enqueueSnapshotDelayed(ctx context.Context) {
+	m.RLock()
+	defer m.RUnlock()
+	for cq := range m.clusterQueues {
+		m.queue.Add(cq)
+	}
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) takeSnapshot(ctx context.Context) {
+	for m.processNextSnapshot(ctx) {
+	}
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) processNextSnapshot(ctx context.Context) bool {
+	m.wm.Lock()
+	defer m.wm.Unlock()
+
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithName("processNextSnapshot")
+
+	key, quit := m.queue.Get()
+	if quit {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	startTime := time.Now()
+	defer func() {
+		log.V(4).Info("Finished snapshot job", "key", key, "elapsed", time.Since(startTime))
+	}()
+
+	cq := m.extractClusterQueue(key)
+	if cq == nil {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	defer m.queue.Done(key)
+
+	workloads := make([]kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload, 0)
+	if elements, ok := cq.Snapshot(m.queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount); ok {
```

  IIUC taking the snapshot here is only protected by the m.wm.Lock, but not by the main m lock. I think this is fine, but I think we need another RW lock at the `clusterQueueBase` level to make sure the `heap` and `inadmissibleWorkloads` are in sync, without a need to take the lock for the entire manager.
  
  @alculquicondor any thoughts?

- **pkg/queue/manager.go:659** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-08-31T08:45:16Z
```diff
@@ -547,3 +594,90 @@ func (m *Manager) reportPendingWorkloads(cqName string, cq ClusterQueue) {
 	}
 	metrics.ReportPendingWorkloads(cqName, active, inadmissible)
 }
+
+func (m *Manager) Start(ctx context.Context) error {
+	defer m.queue.ShutDown()
+
+	queueVisibilityUpdateInterval := time.Duration(m.queueVisibilityUpdateInterval) * time.Second
+
+	for i := 0; i < snapshotWorkers; i++ {
+		go wait.UntilWithContext(ctx, m.takeSnapshot, queueVisibilityUpdateInterval)
+	}
+
+	go wait.UntilWithContext(ctx, m.enqueueSnapshotDelayed, queueVisibilityUpdateInterval)
+
+	<-ctx.Done()
+
+	return nil
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) enqueueSnapshotDelayed(ctx context.Context) {
+	m.RLock()
+	defer m.RUnlock()
+	for cq := range m.clusterQueues {
+		m.queue.Add(cq)
+	}
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) takeSnapshot(ctx context.Context) {
+	for m.processNextSnapshot(ctx) {
+	}
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) processNextSnapshot(ctx context.Context) bool {
+	m.wm.Lock()
+	defer m.wm.Unlock()
+
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithName("processNextSnapshot")
+
+	key, quit := m.queue.Get()
+	if quit {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	startTime := time.Now()
+	defer func() {
+		log.V(4).Info("Finished snapshot job", "key", key, "elapsed", time.Since(startTime))
+	}()
+
+	cq := m.extractClusterQueue(key)
+	if cq == nil {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	defer m.queue.Done(key)
+
+	workloads := make([]kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload, 0)
+	if elements, ok := cq.Snapshot(m.queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount); ok {
+		for _, wl := range elements {
+			workloads = append(workloads, kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload{
+				Name:      wl.Name,
+				Namespace: wl.Namespace,
+			})
+		}
+	}
+	m.snapshots[key.(string)] = workloads
```

  IIUC t is better to have a function on the manager, say `SetSnapshot(cqName, workloads)` and take the lock there.

### Review by [@stuton](https://github.com/stuton) (commented) — 2023-08-31T10:40:05Z

- **pkg/queue/manager.go:659** by [@stuton](https://github.com/stuton) — 2023-08-31T10:40:05Z
```diff
@@ -547,3 +594,90 @@ func (m *Manager) reportPendingWorkloads(cqName string, cq ClusterQueue) {
 	}
 	metrics.ReportPendingWorkloads(cqName, active, inadmissible)
 }
+
+func (m *Manager) Start(ctx context.Context) error {
+	defer m.queue.ShutDown()
+
+	queueVisibilityUpdateInterval := time.Duration(m.queueVisibilityUpdateInterval) * time.Second
+
+	for i := 0; i < snapshotWorkers; i++ {
+		go wait.UntilWithContext(ctx, m.takeSnapshot, queueVisibilityUpdateInterval)
+	}
+
+	go wait.UntilWithContext(ctx, m.enqueueSnapshotDelayed, queueVisibilityUpdateInterval)
+
+	<-ctx.Done()
+
+	return nil
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) enqueueSnapshotDelayed(ctx context.Context) {
+	m.RLock()
+	defer m.RUnlock()
+	for cq := range m.clusterQueues {
+		m.queue.Add(cq)
+	}
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) takeSnapshot(ctx context.Context) {
+	for m.processNextSnapshot(ctx) {
+	}
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) processNextSnapshot(ctx context.Context) bool {
+	m.wm.Lock()
+	defer m.wm.Unlock()
+
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithName("processNextSnapshot")
+
+	key, quit := m.queue.Get()
+	if quit {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	startTime := time.Now()
+	defer func() {
+		log.V(4).Info("Finished snapshot job", "key", key, "elapsed", time.Since(startTime))
+	}()
+
+	cq := m.extractClusterQueue(key)
+	if cq == nil {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	defer m.queue.Done(key)
+
+	workloads := make([]kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload, 0)
+	if elements, ok := cq.Snapshot(m.queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount); ok {
+		for _, wl := range elements {
+			workloads = append(workloads, kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload{
+				Name:      wl.Name,
+				Namespace: wl.Namespace,
+			})
+		}
+	}
+	m.snapshots[key.(string)] = workloads
```

  added function `SetSnapshot(cqName, workloads)`

- **pkg/queue/cluster_queue_impl.go:229** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-09-01T09:25:08Z
```diff
@@ -221,6 +221,21 @@ func (c *clusterQueueBase) DumpInadmissible() (sets.Set[string], bool) {
 	return elements, true
 }
 
+func (c *clusterQueueBase) Snapshot(maxCount int32) ([]*kueue.Workload, bool) {
+	if c.heap.Len() == 0 {
+		return nil, false
+	}
+	elements := make([]*kueue.Workload, 0, c.heap.Len())
+	for i, e := range c.heap.List() {
```

  Please include `inadmissibleWorkloads` in the snapshot. Quoting the two reasons by @alculquicondor from a priv slack:
  - usually all workloads will be in inadmissible, as kueue would be fast to process all jobs until the next job finishes.
  - the inadmissible staging area is more of an implementation detail. It's just a mechanism for us to be able to look at the next elements in the queue.

- **pkg/queue/manager.go:690** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-09-01T09:39:38Z
```diff
@@ -547,3 +594,105 @@ func (m *Manager) reportPendingWorkloads(cqName string, cq ClusterQueue) {
 	}
 	metrics.ReportPendingWorkloads(cqName, active, inadmissible)
 }
+
+func (m *Manager) Start(ctx context.Context) error {
+	defer m.queue.ShutDown()
+
+	queueVisibilityUpdateInterval := time.Duration(m.queueVisibilityUpdateInterval) * time.Second
+
+	for i := 0; i < snapshotWorkers; i++ {
+		go wait.UntilWithContext(ctx, m.takeSnapshot, queueVisibilityUpdateInterval)
+	}
+
+	go wait.UntilWithContext(ctx, m.enqueueSnapshotDelayed, queueVisibilityUpdateInterval)
+
+	<-ctx.Done()
+
+	return nil
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) enqueueSnapshotDelayed(ctx context.Context) {
+	m.RLock()
+	defer m.RUnlock()
+	for cq := range m.clusterQueues {
+		m.queue.Add(cq)
+	}
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) takeSnapshot(ctx context.Context) {
+	for m.processNextSnapshot(ctx) {
+	}
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) processNextSnapshot(ctx context.Context) bool {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithName("processNextSnapshot")
+
+	key, quit := m.queue.Get()
+	if quit {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	startTime := time.Now()
+	defer func() {
+		log.V(4).Info("Finished snapshot job", "key", key, "elapsed", time.Since(startTime))
+	}()
+
+	cq := m.extractClusterQueue(key)
+	if cq == nil {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	defer m.queue.Done(key)
+
+	workloads := make([]kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload, 0)
+	if elements, ok := cq.Snapshot(m.queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount); ok {
+		for _, wl := range elements {
+			workloads = append(workloads, kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload{
+				Name:      wl.Name,
+				Namespace: wl.Namespace,
+			})
+		}
+	}
+	m.SetSnapshot(key.(string), workloads)
+
+	return true
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) extractClusterQueue(key interface{}) ClusterQueue {
+	m.RLock()
+	defer m.RUnlock()
+
+	if len(m.clusterQueues) == 0 {
+		return nil
+	}
+
+	if cq := m.clusterQueues[key.(string)]; cq != nil {
+		return cq
+	}
+
+	return nil
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) SetSnapshot(cqName string, workloads []kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload) {
+	m.wm.Lock()
+	defer m.wm.Unlock()
+	m.snapshots[cqName] = workloads
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) GetSnapshot(cqName string) []kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload {
+	m.wm.RLock()
+	defer m.wm.RUnlock()
+	return m.snapshots[cqName]
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) DeleteSnapshot(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) {
+	m.Lock()
+	defer m.Unlock()
```

  This defer will only end once `DeleteSnapshot` ends, but we can end it ealier. I suggest to extract a function `getClusterQueue` (if there is no already) and take the lock inside this function.

- **pkg/queue/manager.go:648** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-09-01T09:46:16Z
```diff
@@ -547,3 +594,105 @@ func (m *Manager) reportPendingWorkloads(cqName string, cq ClusterQueue) {
 	}
 	metrics.ReportPendingWorkloads(cqName, active, inadmissible)
 }
+
+func (m *Manager) Start(ctx context.Context) error {
+	defer m.queue.ShutDown()
+

+	for i := 0; i < snapshotWorkers; i++ {
+		go wait.UntilWithContext(ctx, m.takeSnapshot, queueVisibilityUpdateInterval)
+	}
+
+	go wait.UntilWithContext(ctx, m.enqueueSnapshotDelayed, queueVisibilityUpdateInterval)
+
+	<-ctx.Done()
+

+}
+
+func (m *Manager) enqueueSnapshotDelayed(ctx context.Context) {
+	m.RLock()
+	defer m.RUnlock()

+		m.queue.Add(cq)
+	}

+func (m *Manager) takeSnapshot(ctx context.Context) {
+	for m.processNextSnapshot(ctx) {
+	}
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) processNextSnapshot(ctx context.Context) bool {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithName("processNextSnapshot")
+
+	key, quit := m.queue.Get()
+	if quit {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	startTime := time.Now()
+	defer func() {
+		log.V(4).Info("Finished snapshot job", "key", key, "elapsed", time.Since(startTime))
+	}()
+
+	cq := m.extractClusterQueue(key)
+	if cq == nil {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	defer m.queue.Done(key)
+
+	workloads := make([]kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload, 0)
+	if elements, ok := cq.Snapshot(m.queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount); ok {
```

  The issue here is that `cq.Snapshot` does not take a lock. This means that `processNextSnapshot` may read inconsistent state of the cq, where the `head.items` and `inadmissibleWorkloads` are inconsistent. There are two solutions:
  1. take the read lock for the entire manager
  2. introduce rw lock at the ClusterQueueBase level
  
  I think 2. is preferred so that we don't need to lock the entire manager, but I guess it can be deferred to a follow up PR. Still, we should address the inconsistency in this PR to avoid race conditions, and I think the rw lock at the ClusterQueueBase level does not sound like much overhead.


  why `wm`? Maybe `sm` for Snapshots Mutex? Or just explicitely `snapshotsMutex`.

### Review by [@stuton](https://github.com/stuton) (commented) — 2023-09-01T15:20:29Z

- **pkg/controller/core/clusterqueue_controller.go:512** by [@stuton](https://github.com/stuton) — 2023-09-01T15:20:29Z

```diff
@@ -497,3 +500,18 @@ func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) updateCqStatusIfChanged(

+
+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) getWorkloadsStatus(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) *kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus {
+	pendingWorkloadsStatus := cq.Status.DeepCopy().PendingWorkloadsStatus
+	if pendingWorkloadsStatus == nil {
```

### Review by [@stuton](https://github.com/stuton) (commented) — 2023-09-01T15:22:33Z

- **pkg/queue/manager.go:690** by [@stuton](https://github.com/stuton) — 2023-09-01T15:22:33Z
```diff
@@ -547,3 +594,105 @@ func (m *Manager) reportPendingWorkloads(cqName string, cq ClusterQueue) {
 	}
 	metrics.ReportPendingWorkloads(cqName, active, inadmissible)
 }
+
+func (m *Manager) Start(ctx context.Context) error {
+	defer m.queue.ShutDown()
+
+	queueVisibilityUpdateInterval := time.Duration(m.queueVisibilityUpdateInterval) * time.Second
+
+	for i := 0; i < snapshotWorkers; i++ {
+		go wait.UntilWithContext(ctx, m.takeSnapshot, queueVisibilityUpdateInterval)
+	}
+
+	go wait.UntilWithContext(ctx, m.enqueueSnapshotDelayed, queueVisibilityUpdateInterval)
+
+	<-ctx.Done()
+
+	return nil
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) enqueueSnapshotDelayed(ctx context.Context) {
+	m.RLock()
+	defer m.RUnlock()
+	for cq := range m.clusterQueues {
+		m.queue.Add(cq)
+	}
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) takeSnapshot(ctx context.Context) {
+	for m.processNextSnapshot(ctx) {
+	}
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) processNextSnapshot(ctx context.Context) bool {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithName("processNextSnapshot")
+
+	key, quit := m.queue.Get()
+	if quit {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	startTime := time.Now()
+	defer func() {
+		log.V(4).Info("Finished snapshot job", "key", key, "elapsed", time.Since(startTime))
+	}()
+
+	cq := m.extractClusterQueue(key)
+	if cq == nil {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	defer m.queue.Done(key)
+
+	workloads := make([]kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload, 0)
+	if elements, ok := cq.Snapshot(m.queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount); ok {
+		for _, wl := range elements {
+			workloads = append(workloads, kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload{
+				Name:      wl.Name,
+				Namespace: wl.Namespace,
+			})
+		}
+	}
+	m.SetSnapshot(key.(string), workloads)
+
+	return true
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) extractClusterQueue(key interface{}) ClusterQueue {
+	m.RLock()
+	defer m.RUnlock()
+
+	if len(m.clusterQueues) == 0 {
+		return nil
+	}
+
+	if cq := m.clusterQueues[key.(string)]; cq != nil {
+		return cq
+	}
+
+	return nil
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) SetSnapshot(cqName string, workloads []kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload) {
+	m.wm.Lock()
+	defer m.wm.Unlock()
+	m.snapshots[cqName] = workloads
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) GetSnapshot(cqName string) []kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload {
+	m.wm.RLock()
+	defer m.wm.RUnlock()
+	return m.snapshots[cqName]
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) DeleteSnapshot(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) {
+	m.Lock()
+	defer m.Unlock()
```

  no need check cq, nothing happens if key won't be exist

```diff
+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) getWorkloadsStatus() *kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus {
+	pendingWorkloads := make([]kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload, 0)
```

```diff
+			clusterQueue = testing.MakeClusterQueue("cluster-queue").

+			workloads := []*kueue.Workload{
+				testing.MakeWorkload("one", ns.Name).Queue(localQueue.Name).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "2").Request(resourceGPU, "2").Obj(),
+				testing.MakeWorkload("two", ns.Name).Queue(localQueue.Name).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "3").Request(resourceGPU, "3").Obj(),
+			}
+
+			ginkgo.By("Creating workloads")
+			for _, w := range workloads {
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, w)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+			}
+			gomega.Eventually(func() *kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus {
+				var updatedCq kueue.ClusterQueue
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(clusterQueue), &updatedCq)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+				return updatedCq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus
+			}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.BeComparableTo(&kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+				Head: []kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload{
+					{
+						Name:      "one",
+						Namespace: ns.Name,
+					},
+					{
+						Name:      "two",
+						Namespace: ns.Name,
+					},
+				},
+			},
+				ignoreLastChangeTime,
+				cmpopts.SortSlices(func(i, j kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload) bool {
```

  Why is this needed? Is it because the workloads `one` and `two` might be created in the same second, and have the same priority, so that they are in random order? I would prefer we don't have this randomness, as it may cover some real issues. I would suggest to use priorities for the workloads to make sure the order is deterministic.

```diff
+
+	for i := 0; i < snapshotWorkers; i++ {
+		go wait.UntilWithContext(ctx, m.takeSnapshot, m.queueVisibilityUpdateInterval)
+	}
+
+	go wait.UntilWithContext(ctx, m.enqueueTakeSnapshot, m.queueVisibilityUpdateInterval)
+
+	<-ctx.Done()
+
+	return nil
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) enqueueTakeSnapshot(ctx context.Context) {
+	m.RLock()
+	defer m.RUnlock()
+	for cq := range m.clusterQueues {
+		m.snapshotsQueue.Add(cq)
+	}
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) takeSnapshot(ctx context.Context) {
+	for m.processNextSnapshot(ctx) {
+	}
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) processNextSnapshot(ctx context.Context) bool {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithName("processNextSnapshot")
+
+	key, quit := m.snapshotsQueue.Get()
+	if quit {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	startTime := time.Now()
+	defer func() {
+		log.V(2).Info("Finished snapshot job", "key", key, "elapsed", time.Since(startTime))
+	}()
+
+	defer m.snapshotsQueue.Done(key)
+
+	workloads := make([]kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload, 0)
+	if elements, ok := m.getSnapshotFromClusterQueue(key); ok {
+		for index, info := range elements {
+			if int32(index) >= m.queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount {
+				break
+			}
+			if info == nil {
+				continue
+			}
+			workloads = append(workloads, kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload{
+				Name:      info.Obj.Name,
+				Namespace: info.Obj.Namespace,
+			})
+		}
+	}
+	m.SetSnapshot(key.(string), workloads)
+
+	return true
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) getSnapshotFromClusterQueue(key interface{}) ([]*workload.Info, bool) {
+	m.RLock()
```

  This lock so for the entire manager (which manages) multiple cluster queues. However, the heaviest operation here is cq.Snapshot, which depends only on one cluster queue. I think, ideally, this operation is not wrapped by `m.RLock`, but the consistency is provided by the lock inside the ClusterQueueBase RWlock (as attempted at some point). I think if this does not go into this PR, there should be a follow up issue created and TODO comment with to follow up at some point.

  Why would we need the `queueOrdering`? IIUC as long as the output is deterministic, we can just expect the certain order in the asserts. My idea is to make the order deterministic by using workload priorities.

```diff
+func (m *Manager) Start(ctx context.Context) error {
+	defer m.queue.ShutDown()

+	}

+

+	for m.processNextSnapshot(ctx) {
+	}

+	if quit {
+		return false

```

### Review by [@stuton](https://github.com/stuton) (commented) — 2023-09-05T10:25:24Z

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2023-09-05T10:35:22Z

- **pkg/queue/cluster_queue_impl.go:225** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-09-05T10:35:22Z
```diff
@@ -221,6 +222,25 @@ func (c *clusterQueueBase) DumpInadmissible() (sets.Set[string], bool) {
 	return elements, true
 }
 
+func (c *clusterQueueBase) Snapshot() ([]*workload.Info, bool) {
```

  I was thinking about returning workloads to keep the API cleaner, as we don't need the other bits of information, such as `TotalRequests` or `ClusterQueue`. It also means GC can cleanup the info objects later. 
  
  However, I now see the tradeoff, that using info allows to save one pass, so feel free to keep as is.

```diff
+			localQueue     *kueue.LocalQueue

+		)
+
```

```diff
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, onDemandFlavor)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+			clusterQueue = testing.MakeClusterQueue("cluster-queue").
+				ResourceGroup(
+					*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas(flavorOnDemand).
+						Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "5", "5").Obj(),
+				).
+				Obj()
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, clusterQueue)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+			localQueue = testing.MakeLocalQueue("queue", ns.Name).ClusterQueue(clusterQueue.Name).Obj()
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, localQueue)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+		})
+
+		ginkgo.AfterEach(func() {
+			util.ExpectClusterQueueToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, clusterQueue, true)
+			util.ExpectResourceFlavorToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, onDemandFlavor, true)
+		})
+
+		ginkgo.It("Should update of the pending workloads when a new workload is scheduled", func() {
+			workloads := []*kueue.Workload{
+				testing.MakeWorkload("one", ns.Name).Queue(localQueue.Name).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "2").Request(resourceGPU, "2").Obj(),
+				testing.MakeWorkload("two", ns.Name).Queue(localQueue.Name).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "3").Request(resourceGPU, "3").Obj(),
+			}
+
+			ginkgo.By("Creating workloads")
+			for _, w := range workloads {
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, w)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+			}
+			gomega.Eventually(func() *kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus {
+				var updatedCq kueue.ClusterQueue
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(clusterQueue), &updatedCq)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+				return updatedCq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus
+			}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.BeComparableTo(&kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+				Head: []kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload{
+					{
+						Name:      "one",
+						Namespace: ns.Name,
+					},
+					{
+						Name:      "two",
+						Namespace: ns.Name,
+					},
+				},
+			},
+				ignoreLastChangeTime,
+				cmpopts.SortSlices(func(i, j kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload) bool {
+					return i.Name < j.Name
+				})))
+
+			ginkgo.By("Creating a new workload")
+			newWorkloads := []*kueue.Workload{
+				testing.MakeWorkload("three", ns.Name).Queue(localQueue.Name).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "2").Request(resourceGPU, "2").Obj(),
+				testing.MakeWorkload("four", ns.Name).Queue(localQueue.Name).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "3").Request(resourceGPU, "3").Obj(),
+			}
+			for _, w := range newWorkloads {
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, w)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+				time.Sleep(time.Second)
+			}
+
+			ginkgo.By("Cut off the head of pending workloads when the number of pending workloads exceeds MaxCount")
+			gomega.Eventually(func() *kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus {
+				var updatedCq kueue.ClusterQueue
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(clusterQueue), &updatedCq)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+				return updatedCq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus
+			}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.BeComparableTo(&kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+				Head: []kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload{
+					{
+						Name:      "one",
+						Namespace: ns.Name,
+					},
+					{
+						Name:      "two",
+						Namespace: ns.Name,
+					},
+					{
+						Name:      "three",
+						Namespace: ns.Name,
+					},
+				},
+			}, ignoreLastChangeTime, cmpopts.SortSlices(func(i, j kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload) bool {
+				return i.Name < j.Name
+			})))
+
+			ginkgo.By("Admitting workloads")
+			admissions := []*kueue.Admission{
+				testing.MakeAdmission(clusterQueue.Name).
+					Assignment(corev1.ResourceCPU, flavorOnDemand, "2").Obj(),
+				testing.MakeAdmission(clusterQueue.Name).
+					Assignment(corev1.ResourceCPU, flavorOnDemand, "3").Obj(),
+				testing.MakeAdmission(clusterQueue.Name).
+					Assignment(corev1.ResourceCPU, flavorOnDemand, "1").Obj(),
+				nil,
+			}
+			for i, w := range workloads {
+				gomega.Eventually(func() error {
+					var newWL kueue.Workload
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(w), &newWL)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+					if admissions[i] != nil {
+						return util.SetQuotaReservation(ctx, k8sClient, &newWL, admissions[i])
+					}
+					return k8sClient.Status().Update(ctx, &newWL)
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			}
+
+			gomega.Eventually(func() *kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus {
+				var updatedCQ kueue.ClusterQueue
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(clusterQueue), &updatedCQ)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+				return updatedCQ.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus
+			}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.BeComparableTo(&kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+				Head: []kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload{
+					{
+						Name:      "three",
+						Namespace: ns.Name,
+					},
+					{
+						Name:      "four",
+						Namespace: ns.Name,
+					},
+				},
+			}, ignoreLastChangeTime, cmpopts.SortSlices(func(i, j kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload) bool {
+				return i.Name < j.Name
+			})))
+
+			ginkgo.By("Finishing workload", func() {
+				util.FinishWorkloads(ctx, k8sClient, workloads...)
+				util.FinishWorkloads(ctx, k8sClient, newWorkloads...)
```

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2023-09-05T12:33:23Z

- **pkg/queue/manager.go:39** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-09-05T12:33:23Z
```diff
@@ -33,6 +36,8 @@ import (
 	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/workload"
 )
 
+const snapshotWorkers = 5
```

  I would keep the manager just as a holder for the snapshots. 
  
  So manager would have only: 
  - snapshots      map[string][]kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload
  - snapshotsMutex sync.RWMutex
  
  Cluster queue manager would have:
  - `snapshotsQueue`
  - `snapshotWorkers`
  - the params: `queueVisibilityUpdateInterval` and `queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount`
  - the Start function
  
  EDIT: the benefits of this are:
  - we make the manager lighter which is shared between multiple components as a dependency
  - we only pass the configuration options   `queueVisibilityUpdateInterval` and `queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount` to clusterqueue controller.
  
  Still, if you encounter some unforeseen complications it is fine as is.

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2023-09-05T14:24:20Z

- **pkg/queue/manager.go:559** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-09-05T14:12:16Z
```diff
@@ -547,3 +552,27 @@ func (m *Manager) reportPendingWorkloads(cqName string, cq ClusterQueue) {
 	}
 	metrics.ReportPendingWorkloads(cqName, active, inadmissible)
 }
+
+func (m *Manager) GetClusterQueues() map[string]ClusterQueue {
+	m.RLock()
+	defer m.RUnlock()
+	return m.clusterQueues
```

  We should not return the map. We need to clone the keys. Returning the map means that the consumer can iterate over the map (unlocked) while another thread is modifying it. Let's have two functions: `GetClusterQueueNames()` and `GetClusterQueue(cqName string)`. Actually, `GetClusterQueue` may not be needed if we have `UpdateSnapshot(cqName) snapshot` which computes the snapshot and sets it.

- **pkg/queue/manager.go:562** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-09-05T14:15:47Z

```diff
 }
+
+func (m *Manager) GetClusterQueues() map[string]ClusterQueue {
+	m.RLock()
+	defer m.RUnlock()
+	return m.clusterQueues
+}
+
+func (m *Manager) SetSnapshot(cqName string, workloads []kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload) {
```

  This is probably not needed if we have `UpdateSnapshot` which computes and saves the snapshot.

- **pkg/controller/core/clusterqueue_controller.go:637** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-09-05T14:18:27Z
```diff
@@ -497,3 +554,93 @@ func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) updateCqStatusIfChanged(
 	}
 	return nil
 }
+
+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) getWorkloadsStatus(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) *kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus {
+	if cq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus == nil {
+		return &kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+			Head:           r.qManager.GetSnapshot(cq.Name),
+			LastChangeTime: metav1.Time{Time: time.Now()},
+		}
+	}
+	if time.Since(cq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus.LastChangeTime.Time) >= r.queueVisibilityUpdateInterval {
+		pendingWorkloads := r.qManager.GetSnapshot(cq.Name)
+		if !equality.Semantic.DeepEqual(cq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus.Head, pendingWorkloads) {
+			return &kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+				Head:           pendingWorkloads,
+				LastChangeTime: metav1.Time{Time: time.Now()},
+			}
+		}
+	}
+	return cq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus
+}
+
+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) Start(ctx context.Context) error {
+	defer r.snapshotsQueue.ShutDown()
+
+	for i := 0; i < snapshotWorkers; i++ {
+		go wait.UntilWithContext(ctx, r.takeSnapshot, r.queueVisibilityUpdateInterval)
+	}
+
+	go wait.UntilWithContext(ctx, r.enqueueTakeSnapshot, r.queueVisibilityUpdateInterval)
+
+	<-ctx.Done()
+
+	return nil
+}
+
+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) enqueueTakeSnapshot(ctx context.Context) {
+	for cq := range r.qManager.GetClusterQueues() {
+		r.snapshotsQueue.Add(cq)
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) takeSnapshot(ctx context.Context) {
+	for r.processNextSnapshot(ctx) {
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) processNextSnapshot(ctx context.Context) bool {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithName("processNextSnapshot")
+
+	key, quit := r.snapshotsQueue.Get()
+	if quit {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	startTime := time.Now()
+	defer func() {
+		log.V(2).Info("Finished snapshot job", "key", key, "elapsed", time.Since(startTime))
+	}()
+
+	defer r.snapshotsQueue.Done(key)
+
+	workloads := make([]kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload, 0)
+	if elements, ok := r.getSnapshotFromClusterQueue(key); ok {
+		for index, info := range elements {
+			if int32(index) >= r.queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount {
+				break
+			}
+			if info == nil {
+				continue
+			}
+			workloads = append(workloads, kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload{
+				Name:      info.Obj.Name,
+				Namespace: info.Obj.Namespace,
+			})
+		}
+	}
+	r.qManager.SetSnapshot(key.(string), workloads)
+
+	return true
+}
+
+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) getSnapshotFromClusterQueue(key interface{}) ([]*workload.Info, bool) {
```

  I think this function does not need to return the bool. Just the list of workloads.

```diff
@@ -221,6 +222,22 @@ func (c *clusterQueueBase) DumpInadmissible() (sets.Set[string], bool) {
 	return elements, true
 }
 
+func (c *clusterQueueBase) Snapshot() ([]*workload.Info, bool) {
```

  This function does not need to return the bool, just the list of workloads

```diff
 	}

+
+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) getWorkloadsStatus(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) *kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus {
+	if cq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus == nil {
+		return &kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+			Head:           r.qManager.GetSnapshot(cq.Name),
+			LastChangeTime: metav1.Time{Time: time.Now()},
+		}
+	}
+	if time.Since(cq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus.LastChangeTime.Time) >= r.queueVisibilityUpdateInterval {
```

  I suggest making this one `if` calling `shouldUpdatePendingWorkloadStatus`. 
  
  Then `shouldUpdatePendingWorkloadStatus` would check `cq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus == nil` OR 
  (`time.Since(cq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus.LastChangeTime.Time) >= r.queueVisibilityUpdateInterval` AND  !equality.Semantic.DeepEqual(cq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus.Head, pendingWorkloads))`
  
  The benefit is that then we have a single place when we create `kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus`.

```diff
 	queueInadmissibleCycle int64

+	rwm sync.RWMutex
```

```diff
 }
+
+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) getWorkloadsStatus(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) *kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus {
+	if cq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus == nil {
+		return &kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+			Head:           r.qManager.GetSnapshot(cq.Name),
+			LastChangeTime: metav1.Time{Time: time.Now()},
+		}
+	}
+	if time.Since(cq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus.LastChangeTime.Time) >= r.queueVisibilityUpdateInterval {
+		pendingWorkloads := r.qManager.GetSnapshot(cq.Name)
+		if !equality.Semantic.DeepEqual(cq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus.Head, pendingWorkloads) {
+			return &kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+				Head:           pendingWorkloads,
+				LastChangeTime: metav1.Time{Time: time.Now()},
+			}
+		}
+	}
+	return cq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus
+}
+
+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) Start(ctx context.Context) error {
+	defer r.snapshotsQueue.ShutDown()
+
+	for i := 0; i < snapshotWorkers; i++ {
+		go wait.UntilWithContext(ctx, r.takeSnapshot, r.queueVisibilityUpdateInterval)
+	}
+
+	go wait.UntilWithContext(ctx, r.enqueueTakeSnapshot, r.queueVisibilityUpdateInterval)
+
+	<-ctx.Done()
+
+	return nil
+}
+
+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) enqueueTakeSnapshot(ctx context.Context) {
+	for cq := range r.qManager.GetClusterQueues() {
+		r.snapshotsQueue.Add(cq)
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) takeSnapshot(ctx context.Context) {
+	for r.processNextSnapshot(ctx) {
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) processNextSnapshot(ctx context.Context) bool {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithName("processNextSnapshot")
+
+	key, quit := r.snapshotsQueue.Get()
+	if quit {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	startTime := time.Now()
+	defer func() {
+		log.V(2).Info("Finished snapshot job", "key", key, "elapsed", time.Since(startTime))
+	}()
+
+	defer r.snapshotsQueue.Done(key)
+
+	workloads := make([]kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload, 0)
+	if elements, ok := r.getSnapshotFromClusterQueue(key); ok {
+		for index, info := range elements {
+			if int32(index) >= r.queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount {
+				break
+			}
+			if info == nil {
+				continue
+			}
+			workloads = append(workloads, kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload{
+				Name:      info.Obj.Name,
+				Namespace: info.Obj.Namespace,
+			})
+		}
+	}
+	r.qManager.SetSnapshot(key.(string), workloads)
+
+	return true
+}
+
+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) getSnapshotFromClusterQueue(key interface{}) ([]*workload.Info, bool) {
+	clusterQueues := r.qManager.GetClusterQueues()
+	if len(clusterQueues) == 0 {
```

  Here we might be checking the state of CQ map, but we no longer have the lock. We should call  `r.qManager.GetClusterQueue(cqName)`. Then, if there is the queue, then we call `cq.Snapshot()` which will take the cq-level lock.

```diff
 			}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(testing.BeNotFoundError())
 		})
 	})

+				).
+				Obj()
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, clusterQueue)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+			localQueue = testing.MakeLocalQueue("queue", ns.Name).ClusterQueue(clusterQueue.Name).Obj()

+			util.ExpectResourceFlavorToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, onDemandFlavor, true)
+		})
```

```diff
+			const lowPrio, midPrio, highPrio = 0, 10, 100
+			workloadsFirstBatch := []*kueue.Workload{
+				testing.MakeWorkload("one", ns.Name).Queue(localQueue.Name).Priority(highPrio).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "2").Request(resourceGPU, "2").Obj(),
+				testing.MakeWorkload("two", ns.Name).Queue(localQueue.Name).Priority(midPrio).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "3").Request(resourceGPU, "3").Obj(),
+			}
+
+			gomega.Eventually(func() *kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus {
+				var updatedCq kueue.ClusterQueue
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(clusterQueue), &updatedCq)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+				return updatedCq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus
+			}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.BeComparableTo(&kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{}, ignoreLastChangeTime))
+
+			ginkgo.By("Creating workloads")
+			for _, w := range workloadsFirstBatch {
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, w)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+			}
+			gomega.Eventually(func() *kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus {
+				var updatedCq kueue.ClusterQueue
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(clusterQueue), &updatedCq)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+				return updatedCq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus
+			}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.BeComparableTo(&kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+				Head: []kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload{
+					{
+						Name:      "one",
+						Namespace: ns.Name,
+					},
+					{
+						Name:      "two",
+						Namespace: ns.Name,
+					},
+				},
+			}, ignoreLastChangeTime))
+
+			ginkgo.By("Creating a new workload")
+			workloadsSecondBatch := []*kueue.Workload{
+				testing.MakeWorkload("three", ns.Name).Queue(localQueue.Name).Priority(midPrio).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "2").Request(resourceGPU, "2").Obj(),
+				testing.MakeWorkload("four", ns.Name).Queue(localQueue.Name).Priority(lowPrio).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "3").Request(resourceGPU, "3").Obj(),
+			}
+			for _, w := range workloadsSecondBatch {
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, w)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+			}
+
+			ginkgo.By("Cut off the head of pending workloads when the number of pending workloads exceeds MaxCount")
```

  ```suggestion
  			ginkgo.By("Verify the head of pending workloads when the number of pending workloads exceeds MaxCount")
  ```
  Will sound better :)

```diff
+				return updatedCq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus
+			}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.BeComparableTo(&kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{}, ignoreLastChangeTime))
+
+			ginkgo.By("Creating workloads")
+			for _, w := range workloadsFirstBatch {
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, w)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+			}
+			gomega.Eventually(func() *kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus {
+				var updatedCq kueue.ClusterQueue
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(clusterQueue), &updatedCq)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+				return updatedCq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus
+			}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.BeComparableTo(&kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+				Head: []kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload{
+					{
+						Name:      "one",
+						Namespace: ns.Name,
+					},
+					{
+						Name:      "two",
+						Namespace: ns.Name,
+					},
+				},
+			}, ignoreLastChangeTime))
+
+			ginkgo.By("Creating a new workload")
+			workloadsSecondBatch := []*kueue.Workload{
+				testing.MakeWorkload("three", ns.Name).Queue(localQueue.Name).Priority(midPrio).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "2").Request(resourceGPU, "2").Obj(),
+				testing.MakeWorkload("four", ns.Name).Queue(localQueue.Name).Priority(lowPrio).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "3").Request(resourceGPU, "3").Obj(),
+			}
+			for _, w := range workloadsSecondBatch {
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, w)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+			}
+
+			ginkgo.By("Cut off the head of pending workloads when the number of pending workloads exceeds MaxCount")
```

  changed here https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/1069/commits/20448ee40ed7f91bb885cdca263f5e10fe1bbe5b

- **pkg/controller/core/clusterqueue_controller.go:588** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-09-06T09:55:15Z
```diff

 	}
 	return nil

+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) getWorkloadsStatus(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) *kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus {
```

- **pkg/controller/core/clusterqueue_controller_test.go:68** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-09-07T10:34:17Z
```diff
@@ -65,6 +65,7 @@ func TestUpdateCqStatusIfChanged(t *testing.T) {
 					Reason:  "FlavorNotFound",
 					Message: "Can't admit new workloads; some flavors are not found",
 				}},
+				PendingWorkloadsStatus: &kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{},
```

  The feature is disabled here so I expect `nil` to be returned actually. Let's adjust the implementation and add a unit test. I suggest to expand this test, but adding a dedicated test case is also fine. If we expand this one the following will need to change:
  - we call `Start` on the Reconciller
  - add extra params to the test case struct: maxCount, updateInterval (existing test cases don't need updates)
  - add test cases for MaxCount=2 & updateInterval=10ms. 
  - When MaxCount>0 the test case should loop await until the snapshot is available by checking `qManager.GetSnapshot(cqName)` periodically, before calling `updateCqStatusIfChanged`

  I think this function should set `nil` if the feature is disabled. I suggest to introduce a helper function `isVisibilityEnabled()` that would check the `MaxCount=0`. Then, use this function here, and in `Start`.

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2023-09-07T13:37:07Z

- **pkg/controller/core/clusterqueue_controller_test.go:566** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-09-07T13:37:07Z
```diff
@@ -489,3 +487,82 @@ func TestRecordResourceMetrics(t *testing.T) {
 		})
 	}
 }
+
+func TestStartSnapshot(t *testing.T) {
+	cqName := "test-cq"
+	lqName := "test-lq"
+	const lowPrio, highPrio = 0, 100
+	defaultWls := &kueue.WorkloadList{
+		Items: []kueue.Workload{
+			*utiltesting.MakeWorkload("one", "").Queue(lqName).Priority(highPrio).Obj(),
+			*utiltesting.MakeWorkload("two", "").Queue(lqName).Priority(lowPrio).Obj(),
+		},
+	}
+	testCases := map[string]struct {
+		queueVisibilityUpdateInterval        time.Duration
+		queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount int32
+		wantPendingWorkloadsStatus           *kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus
+	}{
+		"taking snapshot of cluster queue is disabled": {},
+		"taking snapshot of cluster queue is enabled": {
+			queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount: 2,
+			queueVisibilityUpdateInterval:        10 * time.Millisecond,
+			wantPendingWorkloadsStatus: &kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+				Head: []kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload{
+					{Name: "one"}, {Name: "two"},
+				},
+			},
+		},
+		"verify the head of pending workloads when the number of pending workloads exceeds MaxCount": {
+			queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount: 1,
+			queueVisibilityUpdateInterval:        10 * time.Millisecond,
+			wantPendingWorkloadsStatus: &kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+				Head: []kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload{
+					{Name: "one"},
+				},
+			},
+		},
+	}
+	for name, tc := range testCases {
+		t.Run(name, func(t *testing.T) {
+			cq := utiltesting.MakeClusterQueue(cqName).
+				QueueingStrategy(kueue.StrictFIFO).Obj()
+			lq := utiltesting.MakeLocalQueue(lqName, "").
+				ClusterQueue(cqName).Obj()
+			ctx := context.Background()
+
+			cl := utiltesting.NewClientBuilder().WithLists(defaultWls).WithObjects(lq, cq).WithStatusSubresource(lq, cq).
+				Build()
+			cCache := cache.New(cl)
+			qManager := queue.NewManager(cl, cCache)
+			if err := qManager.AddClusterQueue(ctx, cq); err != nil {
+				t.Fatalf("Inserting clusterQueue in manager: %v", err)
+			}
+			if err := qManager.AddLocalQueue(ctx, lq); err != nil {
+				t.Fatalf("Inserting localQueue in manager: %v", err)
+			}
+
+			r := NewClusterQueueReconciler(
+				cl,
+				qManager,
+				cCache,
+				WithQueueVisibilityUpdateInterval(tc.queueVisibilityUpdateInterval),
+				WithQueueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount(tc.queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount),
+			)
+
+			if err := startSnapshotWithTimeout(ctx, r); err != nil {
+				t.Errorf("error startSnapshotWithTimeout: %v", err)
+			}
+
+			if diff := cmp.Diff(tc.wantPendingWorkloadsStatus, r.getWorkloadsStatus(cq), cmpopts.IgnoreFields(kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{}, "LastChangeTime")); len(diff) != 0 {
+				t.Errorf("unexpected ClusterQueueStatus (-want,+got):\n%s", diff)
+			}
+		})
+	}
+}
+
+func startSnapshotWithTimeout(ctx context.Context, r *ClusterQueueReconciler) error {
+	ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, snapshotTimeout)
+	defer cancel()
```

  IIUC the `defer` should be called outside at the end of test case. Now it would be called when leaving `startSnapshotWithTimeout` which might be too early

  Actually, the cancel function is not of much interest to us here, the main idea to sent a signal "Done" to "Start" function when will "snapshotTimeout" come. It's most similar to "time.Sleep".

```diff
+				Head: []kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload{
+					{Name: "one"},
+				},
+			},
+		},
+	}
+	for name, tc := range testCases {
+		t.Run(name, func(t *testing.T) {
+			cq := utiltesting.MakeClusterQueue(cqName).
+				QueueingStrategy(kueue.StrictFIFO).Obj()
+			lq := utiltesting.MakeLocalQueue(lqName, "").
+				ClusterQueue(cqName).Obj()
+			ctx := context.Background()
+
+			cl := utiltesting.NewClientBuilder().WithLists(defaultWls).WithObjects(lq, cq).WithStatusSubresource(lq, cq).
+				Build()
+			cCache := cache.New(cl)
+			qManager := queue.NewManager(cl, cCache)
+			if err := qManager.AddClusterQueue(ctx, cq); err != nil {
+				t.Fatalf("Inserting clusterQueue in manager: %v", err)

+			if err := qManager.AddLocalQueue(ctx, lq); err != nil {
+				t.Fatalf("Inserting localQueue in manager: %v", err)
+			}

+				t.Errorf("error startSnapshotWithTimeout: %v", err)
+			}
+
```


  Probably, you should be able to repro this by injecting a sleep before `snapshotsQueue.Get`

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2023-09-07T14:49:06Z

- **pkg/controller/core/clusterqueue_controller_test.go:557** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-09-07T14:49:05Z
```diff
@@ -550,19 +551,22 @@ func TestStartSnapshot(t *testing.T) {
 				WithQueueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount(tc.queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount),
 			)
 
-			if err := startSnapshotWithTimeout(ctx, r); err != nil {
-				t.Errorf("error startSnapshotWithTimeout: %v", err)
-			}
+			ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, snapshotTimeout)
+			defer cancel()
+
+			wg := &sync.WaitGroup{}
```

  I'm not sure what is the intention of the block here. I think we should try to follow what normal setup does. I think we want to just call:
  `go r.Start(ctx)`. After that we just wait for the snapshot to be ready by waiting for `qManager.GetSnapshot()`. For waiting we could use `wait.PollUntilContextTimeout`. Let me know if this makes sense.

### Review by [@stuton](https://github.com/stuton) (commented) — 2023-09-07T14:49:15Z

```diff
+func TestStartSnapshot(t *testing.T) {
+	cqName := "test-cq"
+	lqName := "test-lq"
+	const lowPrio, highPrio = 0, 100
+	defaultWls := &kueue.WorkloadList{
+		Items: []kueue.Workload{
+			*utiltesting.MakeWorkload("one", "").Queue(lqName).Priority(highPrio).Obj(),
+			*utiltesting.MakeWorkload("two", "").Queue(lqName).Priority(lowPrio).Obj(),
+		},
+	}
+	testCases := map[string]struct {
+		queueVisibilityUpdateInterval        time.Duration
+		queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount int32
+		wantPendingWorkloadsStatus           *kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus
+	}{
+		"taking snapshot of cluster queue is disabled": {},
+		"taking snapshot of cluster queue is enabled": {
+			queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount: 2,
+			queueVisibilityUpdateInterval:        10 * time.Millisecond,
+			wantPendingWorkloadsStatus: &kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+				Head: []kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload{
+					{Name: "one"}, {Name: "two"},
+				},
+			},
+		},
+		"verify the head of pending workloads when the number of pending workloads exceeds MaxCount": {
+			queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount: 1,
+			queueVisibilityUpdateInterval:        10 * time.Millisecond,
+			wantPendingWorkloadsStatus: &kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+				Head: []kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload{
+					{Name: "one"},
+				},
+			},
+		},
+	}
+	for name, tc := range testCases {
+		t.Run(name, func(t *testing.T) {
+			cq := utiltesting.MakeClusterQueue(cqName).
+				QueueingStrategy(kueue.StrictFIFO).Obj()
+			lq := utiltesting.MakeLocalQueue(lqName, "").
+				ClusterQueue(cqName).Obj()
+			ctx := context.Background()
+
+			cl := utiltesting.NewClientBuilder().WithLists(defaultWls).WithObjects(lq, cq).WithStatusSubresource(lq, cq).
+				Build()
+			cCache := cache.New(cl)
+			qManager := queue.NewManager(cl, cCache)
+			if err := qManager.AddClusterQueue(ctx, cq); err != nil {
+				t.Fatalf("Inserting clusterQueue in manager: %v", err)
+			}
+			if err := qManager.AddLocalQueue(ctx, lq); err != nil {
+				t.Fatalf("Inserting localQueue in manager: %v", err)
+			}
+
+			r := NewClusterQueueReconciler(
+				cl,
+				qManager,
+				cCache,
+				WithQueueVisibilityUpdateInterval(tc.queueVisibilityUpdateInterval),
+				WithQueueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount(tc.queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount),
+			)
+
+			if err := startSnapshotWithTimeout(ctx, r); err != nil {
+				t.Errorf("error startSnapshotWithTimeout: %v", err)
+			}
+
+			if diff := cmp.Diff(tc.wantPendingWorkloadsStatus, r.getWorkloadsStatus(cq), cmpopts.IgnoreFields(kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{}, "LastChangeTime")); len(diff) != 0 {
+				t.Errorf("unexpected ClusterQueueStatus (-want,+got):\n%s", diff)
+			}
+		})
+	}
+}
+
+func startSnapshotWithTimeout(ctx context.Context, r *ClusterQueueReconciler) error {
+	ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, snapshotTimeout)
+	defer cancel()
```

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2023-09-07T15:19:22Z

- **pkg/controller/core/clusterqueue_controller_test.go:557** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-09-07T15:19:22Z
```diff
@@ -550,19 +551,22 @@ func TestStartSnapshot(t *testing.T) {
 				WithQueueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount(tc.queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount),
 			)
 
-			if err := startSnapshotWithTimeout(ctx, r); err != nil {
-				t.Errorf("error startSnapshotWithTimeout: %v", err)
-			}
+			ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, snapshotTimeout)
+			defer cancel()
+
+			wg := &sync.WaitGroup{}
```

  To be more precise, I don't think we need the `snapshotTimeout`. One way to wait for the expected status is also 
  ```golang
  	diff := ""
  	if err := wait.PollUntilContextTimeout(ctx, time.Second, time.Minute, false, func(ctx context.Context) (done bool, err error) {
  		diff = cmp.Diff(tc.wantPendingWorkloadsStatus, r.getWorkloadsStatus(cq), cmpopts.IgnoreFields(kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{}, "LastChangeTime"))
  		return diff == "", nil
  	}); err != nil {
  		t.Fatalf("Failed to get snapshot computed, last diff=%s", diff)
  	}
  ```

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2023-09-07T15:23:26Z

- **pkg/controller/core/clusterqueue_controller.go:567** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-09-07T15:23:25Z
```diff
@@ -497,3 +552,74 @@ func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) updateCqStatusIfChanged(
 	}
 	return nil
 }
+
+// Taking snapshot of cluster queue is enabled when maxcount non-zero
+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) isVisibilityEnabled() bool {
+	return r.queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount > 0
+}
+
+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) getWorkloadsStatus(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) *kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus {
+	if !r.isVisibilityEnabled() {
+		return nil
+	}
+	if r.shouldUpdatePendingWorkloadStatus(cq) {
+		return &kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+			Head:           r.qManager.GetSnapshot(cq.Name),
```

  Here is actually a small performance issue we may fix in follow up, as this code may compute the snapshot twice: 
  - once to check the condition, and once to put the head. 
  I guess, we could do only the initial checking by `cq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus == nil || time.Since(cq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus.LastChangeTime.Time) >= r.queueVisibilityUpdateInterval`. If this check pass we need to compute the snapshot and reuse as value.

```diff
+				Head: []kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload{
+					{Name: "one"}, {Name: "two"},
+				},
+			},
+		},
+		"verify the head of pending workloads when the number of pending workloads exceeds MaxCount": {
+			queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount: 1,
+			queueVisibilityUpdateInterval:        10 * time.Millisecond,
+			wantPendingWorkloadsStatus: &kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+				Head: []kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkload{
+					{Name: "one"},
+				},
+			},
+		},
+	}
+	for name, tc := range testCases {
+		t.Run(name, func(t *testing.T) {
+			cq := utiltesting.MakeClusterQueue(cqName).
+				QueueingStrategy(kueue.StrictFIFO).Obj()
+			lq := utiltesting.MakeLocalQueue(lqName, "").
+				ClusterQueue(cqName).Obj()
+			ctx := context.Background()
+
+			cl := utiltesting.NewClientBuilder().WithLists(defaultWls).WithObjects(lq, cq).WithStatusSubresource(lq, cq).
+				Build()
+			cCache := cache.New(cl)
+			qManager := queue.NewManager(cl, cCache)
+			if err := qManager.AddClusterQueue(ctx, cq); err != nil {
+				t.Fatalf("Inserting clusterQueue in manager: %v", err)
+			}
+			if err := qManager.AddLocalQueue(ctx, lq); err != nil {
+				t.Fatalf("Inserting localQueue in manager: %v", err)
+			}
+
+			r := NewClusterQueueReconciler(
+				cl,
+				qManager,
+				cCache,
+				WithQueueVisibilityUpdateInterval(tc.queueVisibilityUpdateInterval),
+				WithQueueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount(tc.queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount),
+			)
+
+			go func() {
+				if err := r.Start(ctx); err != nil {
+					t.Errorf("error start snapshot: %v", err)
```

  ```suggestion
  					t.Errorf("error starting the cluster queue reconciler: %v", err)
  ```

```diff
+	rfUpdateCh                           chan event.GenericEvent
+	watchers                             []ClusterQueueUpdateWatcher
+	reportResourceMetrics                bool
+	queueVisibilityUpdateInterval        time.Duration
+	queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount int32
+}
+
+type ClusterQueueReconcilerOptions struct {
+	Watchers                             []ClusterQueueUpdateWatcher
+	ReportResourceMetrics                bool
+	QueueVisibilityUpdateInterval        time.Duration
+	QueueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount int32
+}
+
+// Option configures the reconciler.
+type ClusterQueueReconcilerOption func(*ClusterQueueReconcilerOptions)
+
+func WithWatchers(watchers ...ClusterQueueUpdateWatcher) ClusterQueueReconcilerOption {
+	return func(o *ClusterQueueReconcilerOptions) {
+		o.Watchers = watchers
+	}

+func WithReportResourceMetrics(report bool) ClusterQueueReconcilerOption {
+	return func(o *ClusterQueueReconcilerOptions) {
+		o.ReportResourceMetrics = report
+	}
+}
+
+// WithQueueVisibilityUpdateInterval specifies the time interval for updates to the structure
+// of the top pending workloads in the queues.
+func WithQueueVisibilityUpdateInterval(interval time.Duration) ClusterQueueReconcilerOption {
+	return func(o *ClusterQueueReconcilerOptions) {
+		o.QueueVisibilityUpdateInterval = interval
+	}
 }
 
+// WithQueueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount indicates the maximal number of pending workloads exposed in the
+// cluster queue status
+func WithQueueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount(value int32) ClusterQueueReconcilerOption {
+	return func(o *ClusterQueueReconcilerOptions) {
+		o.QueueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount = value
+	}
+}
+
+var DefaultOptions = ClusterQueueReconcilerOptions{}
```

  Does it need to be exported?

- **pkg/controller/core/clusterqueue_controller.go:583** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-09-07T20:38:09Z
```diff
@@ -497,3 +552,77 @@ func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) updateCqStatusIfChanged(
 	}
 	return nil
 }
+
+// Taking snapshot of cluster queue is enabled when maxcount non-zero
+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) isVisibilityEnabled() bool {
+	return r.queueVisibilityClusterQueuesMaxCount > 0
+}
+
+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) getWorkloadsStatus(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) *kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus {
+	if !r.isVisibilityEnabled() {
+		return nil
+	}
+	if cq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus == nil {
+		return &kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+			Head:           r.qManager.GetSnapshot(cq.Name),
+			LastChangeTime: metav1.Time{Time: time.Now()},
+		}
+	}
+	if time.Since(cq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus.LastChangeTime.Time) >= r.queueVisibilityUpdateInterval {
+		pendingWorkloads := r.qManager.GetSnapshot(cq.Name)
+		if !equality.Semantic.DeepEqual(cq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus.Head, pendingWorkloads) {
+			return &kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+				Head:           pendingWorkloads,
+				LastChangeTime: metav1.Time{Time: time.Now()},
+			}
+		}
+	}
+	return cq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus
+}
+
+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) Start(ctx context.Context) error {
```

  what calls this function? Is it internally called within `SetupWithManager`?
  
  It feels a bit like an overload to make the Reconciler also be the one that calls the reconciler? If possible, I would split it into its own struct.

- **pkg/queue/cluster_queue_impl.go:258** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-09-07T20:41:14Z
```diff
@@ -221,7 +244,27 @@ func (c *clusterQueueBase) DumpInadmissible() (sets.Set[string], bool) {
 	return elements, true
 }
 
+func (c *clusterQueueBase) Snapshot() []*workload.Info {
+	c.rwm.RLock()
+	defer c.rwm.RUnlock()
+	totalLen := c.heap.Len() + len(c.inadmissibleWorkloads)
+	elements := make([]*workload.Info, 0, totalLen)
+	for _, e := range c.heap.List() {
+		info := e.(*workload.Info)
+		elements = append(elements, info)
+	}
+	for _, e := range c.inadmissibleWorkloads {
+		elements = append(elements, e)
+	}
```

  could we release the lock at this point?

```diff
+
+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) getWorkloadsStatus(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) *kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus {
+	if !r.isVisibilityEnabled() {
+		return nil
+	}
+	if cq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus == nil {
+		return &kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+			Head:           r.qManager.GetSnapshot(cq.Name),
+			LastChangeTime: metav1.Time{Time: time.Now()},
+		}
+	}
+	if time.Since(cq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus.LastChangeTime.Time) >= r.queueVisibilityUpdateInterval {
+		pendingWorkloads := r.qManager.GetSnapshot(cq.Name)
+		if !equality.Semantic.DeepEqual(cq.Status.PendingWorkloadsStatus.Head, pendingWorkloads) {
+			return &kueue.ClusterQueuePendingWorkloadsStatus{
+				Head:           pendingWorkloads,
+				LastChangeTime: metav1.Time{Time: time.Now()},
+			}
+		}
+	}

+}
+
+func (r *ClusterQueueReconciler) Start(ctx context.Context) error {
```

  I have traced this a little. The `clusterqueue_controller.Start` is called from here: https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/controller-runtime/blob/2a553d6f910dfc4b0796142ba1e059639a21c54a/pkg/manager/runnable_group.go#L223C17-L223C22.
  
  So, the `Start` is registered in the runnable `Other` group here, and Started here:  https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/controller-runtime/blob/2a553d6f910dfc4b0796142ba1e059639a21c54a/pkg/manager/internal.go#L417.
  
  The start we call from within Kueue: https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/blob/330505e44fd2d6bbfecd708755ba81f59d14906b/cmd/kueue/main.go#L175.
  
  So calling `SetupWithManager` does not call directly the `Start`, but registers the runnable.
  
  I see, seems possible. There could be something like `ClusterQueueSnapshotManager`.
